**:skip** - *Force skip the current song.*
**:leave-voice** - *Leaves the voice channel.*

**:request** - *Request a song via a youtube or soundcloud link, or any kind of compatible music file.*
**:music pause** - *Pauses the current song.*
**:music play** - *Resumes the current song.*
**:volume** - *Change the volume of the current song.*

**:skip** - *Force skip the current song.*
**:leave-voice** - *Leaves the voice channel.*

**:music play** - *Resumes the current song.*
**:volume** - *Change the volume of the current song.*
**:playlist** - *List upcoming requested songs.*
**:shuffle** - *Shuffle the music playlist.*
**:voteskip** - *Vote to skip the current song.*
**:skip** - *Force skip the current song.*
**:leave-voice** - *Leaves the voice channel.*

__**Voice Commands**__
**:request** - *Request a song via a youtube or soundcloud link, or any kind of compatible music file.*
**:music pause** - *Pauses the current song.*
**:music play** - *Resumes the current song.*
**:volume** - *Change the volume of the current song.*
**:playlist** - *List upcoming requested songs.*
**:shuffle** - *Shuffle the music playlist.*
**:voteskip** - *Vote to skip the current song.*
**:skip** - *Force skip the current song.*
**:leave-voice** - *Leaves the voice channel.*
